May 18, 2020 Photo credit WBEN/Mike Baggerman By Mike Baggerman October 7, 2020 10/07/2020 4:45 pm BUFFALO, N.Y. (WBEN) \xe2\x80\x93 Western New York reported a 0.9 percent infection rate, according to Governor Andrew Cuomo during a Wednesday news conference. \xe2\x80\x9cIt\xe2\x80\x99s a good number in general but especially good for Western New York,\xe2\x80\x9d Cuomo said. The infection rate for October 6 was the lowest for the region since September 22. New York\xe2\x80\x99s positive test rate was 1 percent across the entire state. Cuomo said the \xe2\x80\x9chotspots\xe2\x80\x9d are five times that of the overall state rate and predominantly in New York City. \xe2\x80\x9cThe spread is inevitable if we do not control the hotspots,\xe2\x80\x9d Cuomo said. \xe2\x80\x9cThere are facts, even if they\xe2\x80\x99re unpleasant and we know, because we have lived it and every expert will tell you and our experience shows it, if you do not control the infection rate, it will spread.\xe2\x80\x9d Related Cuomo announces \'Cluster Action Initiative\' The governor doubled down on his cluster initiative that would effectively shut down non-essential businesses and limit gatherings in any area where there is deemed to be a cluster by the state. Protesters in New York City blasted the initiative and a demonstration Orthodox Jewish worshippers on Tuesday night featured burning of masks in response to the state plan. \xe2\x80\x9cThere are communities that are upset, that\xe2\x80\x99s because they haven\xe2\x80\x99t been following the original rules,\xe2\x80\x9d Cuomo said. \xe2\x80\x9cThat\xe2\x80\x99s why the infection spread because they weren\xe2\x80\x99t following the rules. The rules weren\xe2\x80\x99t being enforced and they weren\xe2\x80\x99t being enforced because the community didn\xe2\x80\x99t want to follow them. That\xe2\x80\x99s why we are where we are. Make no mistake.\xe2\x80\x9d Cuomo said the rules are a \xe2\x80\x9cdramatic shift\xe2\x80\x9d in society but defended his actions by saying it was data-driven and not arbitrary against any community. The governor also blasted President Trump on Thursday for the federal government\xe2\x80\x99s decision not to address a stimulus bill until after the election. He called it the \xe2\x80\x9cheight of unreasonableness.\xe2\x80\x9d \xe2\x80\x9cThe only way to get close to closing that ($50 billion deficit) within the state\xe2\x80\x99s abilities, you would have to do a tax increase, you would have to cut expenses, and you would have to borrow,\xe2\x80\x9d Cuomo said. \xe2\x80\x9cThis would do tremendous economic damage to the state. My position is the state is not liable for this deficit. It was caused by the federal government\xe2\x80\x99s negligence. I\xe2\x80\x99m not taking action to close the deficit.
